## Basics
*Complete the basic topics in the given order to get started with Competitive Programming.*

### Intro to Programming
#### What is Programming?
- **Topic ID**: `programming`
- **Difficulty**: Basic
- **Importance**: High
- **Phase**: Phase 0
- **Interview Topic**: Yes

**C++ Resources**:
- [Why Programming Is Important? |  Bugra Kilic](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Dv7gLpW91DM) ⭐ 🎥
  - [What is Coding?  | TeXplaiNIT](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=N7ZmPYaXoic) ⭐ 🎥
  - [What is Programming? | Code Academy](https://www.codecademy.com/article/what-is-programming)
  - [What is Computer Programming? | freecodecamp](https://www.freecodecamp.org/news/what-is-programming/) ⭐

**Python Resources**:
*The concept and algorithmic implementation remain identical in Python. Refer to the general resources above.*

**Practice Problems**:
- No practice problems mapped to this topic.

### Learn a Language
*Learning C++ is recommended.*

- **Difficulty**: Basic
- **Importance**: High
- **Phase**: Phase 0
- **Interview Topic**: Yes

  - [Virtual Judge](https://vjudge.net/) ⭐ *(Create an account here, we will practice some problems on this judge. You can submit your code and test if your code is right or wrong automatically.)*

#### Maximum Independent Set (MIS)
- **Topic ID**: `maximum_independent_set`
- **Difficulty**: Medium
- **Importance**: High
- **Phase**: Not Specified
- **Interview Topic**: No
- **Description**: Note that the MIS is the complement of the Maximum Clique. So you can solve the MIS problem by solving the Maximum Clique problem.

#### Linear Diophantine With N Unknowns and Two Equations
- **Topic ID**: `linear_diophantine_with_n_unknowns_and_two_equations`
- **Difficulty**: Medium
- **Importance**: Low
- **Phase**: Not Specified
- **Interview Topic**: No
- **Description**: Given two arrays a and b of length n <= 10^5, and two integers p and q. Check if there exists an array x of length n such that the following equations are satisfied:
                        sum(x[i] * a[i]) = p,
                        sum(x[i] * b[i]) = q,
                        x[i]s can only be integers.

#### [Trick] Linear Combination of Vectors
- **Topic ID**: `linear_combination_of_vectors`
- **Difficulty**: Medium
- **Importance**: Medium
- **Phase**: Not Specified
- **Interview Topic**: No
- **Description**: For n vectors v1, v2, ..., vn, if we plot all the points a1*v1 + a2*v2 + ... + an*vn, where a1+a2+...+an=1, we get a convex polygon of the given points.

**Practice Problems**:
- [Chemistry Lab](https://codeforces.com/problemset/problem/1765/F) (ID: `codeforces_1765f` | Difficulty: Medium ⭐)

#### [Problem] Circle/Polygon Inclusion Tree
- **Topic ID**: `circle_inclusion_hierarchy`
- **Difficulty**: Hard
- **Importance**: Low
- **Phase**: Not Specified
- **Interview Topic**: No
- **Description**: Given n non-intersecting circles/polygons. Some circles can be inside of others. Make a tree such that if 
            𝑖-th circle is inside of 𝑗-th circle, the 𝑖-th vertex is in the subtree of 𝑗-th vertex.

**Practice Problems**:
- [Freedom from Prison](https://codeforces.com/gym/103388/problem/F) (ID: `cf_gym_103388f` | Difficulty: Hard ⭐)
- [Bomas](https://open.kattis.com/problems/bomas) (ID: `kattis_bomas` | Difficulty: Medium ⭐)

#### Birthday Paradox
- **Topic ID**: `birthday_paradox`
- **Difficulty**: Medium
- **Importance**: Low
- **Phase**: Not Specified
- **Interview Topic**: No
- **Description**: If you pick a random number from 1 to x, then after around O(sqrt(x)) picks, you will have a 50% chance of getting a duplicate.
